### <a id="the-inductive-types-h-s-p-v">The Inductive Types H, S, P, V</a>

This section presents the [Varieties.Varieties][] module of the [Agda Universal Algebra Library][].

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="329" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="333" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="341" class="Pragma">--without-K</a> <a id="353" class="Pragma">--exact-split</a> <a id="367" class="Pragma">--safe</a> <a id="374" class="Symbol">#-}</a>

<a id="379" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="384" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="391" href="Algebras.Signatures.html" class="Module">Algebras.Signatures</a> <a id="411" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="417" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="418" href="Algebras.Signatures.html#1299" class="Function">Signature</a><a id="427" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="429" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#5600" class="Generalizable">𝓞</a><a id="430" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="432" href="Universes.html#262" class="Generalizable">𝓥</a><a id="433" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="435" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="440" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="447" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html" class="Module">MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems</a> <a id="473" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="479" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="480" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html#3468" class="Function">global-dfunext</a><a id="494" class="Symbol">)</a>


<a id="498" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="505" href="Varieties.Varieties.html" class="Module">Varieties.Varieties</a> <a id="525" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="526" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a> <a id="528" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="530" href="Algebras.Signatures.html#1299" class="Function">Signature</a> <a id="540" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#5600" class="Generalizable">𝓞</a> <a id="542" href="Universes.html#262" class="Generalizable">𝓥</a><a id="543" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="545" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#545" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="549" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="551" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html#3468" class="Function">global-dfunext</a><a id="565" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="567" class="Keyword">where</a>

<a id="574" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="579" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="586" href="Varieties.EquationalLogic.html" class="Module">Varieties.EquationalLogic</a><a id="611" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="612" class="Argument">𝑆</a> <a id="614" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="616" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="617" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="619" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#545" class="Bound">gfe</a><a id="622" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="624" class="Keyword">public</a>
<a id="631" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="636" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="643" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html" class="Module">MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems</a> <a id="669" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="675" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="676" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a><a id="683" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="685" class="Comment">-- public</a>

</pre>


Fix a signature 𝑆, let 𝒦 be a class of 𝑆-algebras, and define

* H 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a homomorphic image of a members of 𝒦;
* S 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a subalgebra of a member of 𝒦;
* P 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a product of members of 𝒦.

A straight-forward verification confirms that H, S, and P are **closure operators** (expansive, monotone, and idempotent).  A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is said to be *closed under the taking of homomorphic images* provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. Similarly, 𝒦 is *closed under the taking of subalgebras* (resp., *arbitrary products*) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` (resp., `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`). The operators H, S, and P can be composed with one another repeatedly, forming yet more closure operators.

An algebra is a homomorphic image (resp., subalgebra; resp., product) of every algebra to which it is isomorphic. Thus, the class `H 𝒦` (resp., `S 𝒦`; resp., `P 𝒦`) is closed under isomorphism.

A **variety** is a class of algebras, in the same signature, that is closed under the taking of homomorphic images, subalgebras, and arbitrary products.  To represent varieties we define inductive types for the closure operators `H`, `S`, and `P` that are composable.  Separately, we define an inductive type `V` which simultaneously represents closure under all three operators, `H`, `S`, and `P`.




#### <a id="homomorphic-closure">Homomorphic closure</a>

We define the inductive type `H` to represent classes of algebras that include all homomorphic images of algebras in the class; i.e., classes that are closed under the taking of homomorphic images.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="2296" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="H"></a><a id="2301" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2301" class="Datatype">H</a> <a id="2303" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2304" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2304" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="2306" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2306" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="2308" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2310" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="2318" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="2320" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2320" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="2322" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2324" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="2329" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2330" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="2338" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2304" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="2340" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="2341" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="2343" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="2346" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2304" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="2347" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="2350" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="2353" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="2358" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2359" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="2367" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2368" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2304" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="2370" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="2372" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2306" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="2373" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2375" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="2376" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="2378" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a><a id="2380" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2381" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2304" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="2383" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="2385" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2306" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="2386" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="2389" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="H.hlift"></a><a id="2454" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2454" class="InductiveConstructor">hlift</a> <a id="2460" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2462" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2463" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2463" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="2465" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2467" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="2475" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2304" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="2477" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="2478" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2480" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2482" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2463" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="2484" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="2486" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2301" class="Datatype">H</a><a id="2487" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2488" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2304" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="2489" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="2491" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2304" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="2492" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2494" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2320" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="2496" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2498" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4673" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="2507" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2463" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="2509" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2306" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="2511" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="2513" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2301" class="Datatype">H</a> <a id="2515" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2320" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

#### <a id="subalgebraic-closure">Subalgebraic closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing the semantic notion of a class of algebras that is closed under the taking of subalgebras is the following.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="2939" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="S"></a><a id="2944" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2944" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="2946" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2947" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2947" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="2949" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2949" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="2951" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2953" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="2961" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="2963" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2963" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="2965" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2967" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="2972" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2973" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="2981" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2947" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="2983" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="2984" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2986" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2987" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="2990" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2947" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="2991" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="2994" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="2997" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3002" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3003" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3011" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3012" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2947" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3014" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3016" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2949" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3017" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3019" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3020" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3022" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3023" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a><a id="3025" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3026" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2947" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3028" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3030" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2949" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3031" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3034" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="S.sbase"></a><a id="3042" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3042" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="3048" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3050" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3051" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3051" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3053" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3055" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3063" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2947" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3065" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3066" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3068" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3070" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3051" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3072" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3074" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2963" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="3076" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3078" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4673" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="3087" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3051" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3089" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2949" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="3091" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3093" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2944" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="3095" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2963" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="S.slift"></a><a id="3099" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3099" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a> <a id="3105" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3107" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3108" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3108" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3110" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3112" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3120" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2947" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3122" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3123" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3125" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3127" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3108" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3129" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3131" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2944" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="3132" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3133" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2947" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="3134" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="3136" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2947" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="3137" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3139" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2963" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="3141" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3143" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4673" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="3152" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3108" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3154" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2949" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="3156" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3158" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2944" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="3160" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2963" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

  <a id="S.ssubw"></a><a id="3243" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3243" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a> <a id="3249" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3251" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3252" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3252" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3254" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3254" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="3256" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3258" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3266" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="3268" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3269" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3271" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3273" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3252" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3275" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3277" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2944" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="3278" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3279" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2947" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="3280" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="3282" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2949" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3283" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3285" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2963" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="3287" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3289" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3254" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="3291" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3598" class="Function Operator">≤</a> <a id="3293" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3252" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3295" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3297" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3254" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="3299" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3301" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2944" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="3303" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2963" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="product-closure">Product closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing the semantic notion of an class of algebras closed under the taking of arbitrary products is the following.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3639" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="P"></a><a id="3644" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3644" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="3646" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3647" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4093" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4095" href="Algebras.Products.html#908" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="4097" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4044" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="4099" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4101" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3644" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4103" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3663" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="P.pisou"></a><a id="4107" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4107" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a>  <a id="4114" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4116" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4117" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4117" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4119" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4121" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4129" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3647" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4131" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4132" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4134" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4134" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4136" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4138" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4146" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="4148" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4149" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4151" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4153" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4117" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4155" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4157" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3644" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4158" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4159" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3647" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4160" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4162" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3647" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4163" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4165" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3663" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4167" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4169" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4117" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4171" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1151" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4173" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4134" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4175" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4177" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4134" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4179" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4181" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3644" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4183" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3663" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="P.pisow"></a><a id="4187" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4187" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a>  <a id="4194" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4196" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4197" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4197" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4199" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4199" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4201" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4203" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4211" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="4213" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4214" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4216" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4218" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4197" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4220" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4222" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3644" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4223" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4224" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3647" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4225" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4227" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3649" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4228" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4230" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3663" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4232" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4234" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4197" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4236" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1151" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4238" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4199" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4240" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4242" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4199" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4244" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4246" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3644" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4248" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3663" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="varietal-closure">Varietal closure</a>

A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is called a **variety** if it is closed under each of the closure operators H, S, and P introduced above; the corresponding closure operator is often denoted 𝕍, but we will denote it by `V`.

We now define `V` as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="4588" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="V"></a><a id="4593" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4593" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="4595" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4596" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4596" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4598" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4598" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="4600" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4602" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="4610" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="4612" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4612" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4614" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4616" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="4621" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4622" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4630" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4596" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4632" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4633" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="4635" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="4638" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4596" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4639" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="4642" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="4645" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="4650" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4651" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4659" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4660" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4596" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4662" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4664" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4598" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4665" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4667" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4668" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="4670" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a><a id="4672" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4673" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4596" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4675" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4677" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4598" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4678" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="4681" class="Keyword">where</a>

href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5201" class="Bound">I</a> <a id="5216" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5218" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5226" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5228" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5229" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5231" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5233" class="Symbol">(∀</a> <a id="5236" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5236" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="5238" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5240" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5241" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5210" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="5243" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5236" class="Bound">i</a><a id="5244" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5246" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5248" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4593" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5249" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5250" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4596" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5251" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5253" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4598" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5254" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5256" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4612" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="5257" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5259" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5261" href="Algebras.Products.html#908" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="5263" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5210" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="5265" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5267" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4593" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5269" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4612" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="V.visou"></a><a id="5273" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5273" class="InductiveConstructor">visou</a>  <a id="5280" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5282" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5283" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5283" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5285" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5287" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5295" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4596" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5297" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5298" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5300" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5300" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5302" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5304" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5312" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5314" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5315" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5317" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5319" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5283" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5321" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5323" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4593" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5324" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5325" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4596" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5326" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5328" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4596" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5329" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5331" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4612" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5333" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5335" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5283" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5337" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1151" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="5339" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5300" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5341" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5343" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5300" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5345" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5347" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4593" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5349" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4612" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="V.visow"></a><a id="5353" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5353" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a>  <a id="5360" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5362" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5363" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5363" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5365" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5365" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5367" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5369" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5377" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5379" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5380" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5382" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5384" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5363" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5386" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5388" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4593" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5389" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5390" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4596" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5391" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5393" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4598" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5394" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5396" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4612" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5398" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5400" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5363" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5402" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1151" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="5404" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5365" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5406" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5408" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5365" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5410" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5412" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4593" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5414" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4612" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

Thus, if 𝒦 is a class of 𝑆-algebras, then the **variety generated by** 𝒦 is denoted by `V 𝒦` and defined to be the smallest class that contains 𝒦 and is closed under `H`, `S`, and `P`.

With the closure operator V representing closure under HSP, we represent formally what it means to be a variety of algebras as follows.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="is-variety"></a><a id="5766" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5766" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="5777" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5779" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5780" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5780" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5782" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5784" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="5792" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="5794" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5794" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5796" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5798" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5803" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5804" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5812" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5780" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5814" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5815" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5817" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5820" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5780" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5821" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5824" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5826" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5829" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5780" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5831" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="5833" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5766" class="Function">is-variety</a><a id="5843" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5844" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5844" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5845" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5847" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5847" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5849" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5851" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4593" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5852" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5853" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5844" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5854" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5856" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5844" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5857" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5859" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5847" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5861" href="Relations.Unary.html#2280" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="5863" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5847" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

<a id="variety"></a><a id="5866" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5866" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="5874" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5876" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5877" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5877" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5879" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5881" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="5889" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5891" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5893" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5894" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5897" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5877" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5898" class="Symbol">)</a><a id="5899" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a> <a id="5901" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="5903" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5866" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="5911" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5911" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5913" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5915" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="5917" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5917" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5919" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="5921" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5922" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5927" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5928" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5936" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5911" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5938" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5939" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5941" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5944" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5911" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5945" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5948" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="5950" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5766" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="5961" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5917" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="V-is-closed-under-lift">V is closed under lift</a>

As mentioned earlier, a technical hurdle that must be overcome when formalizing proofs in Agda is the proper handling of universe levels. In particular, in the proof of the Birkhoff's theorem, for example, we will need to know that if an algebra 𝑨 belongs to the variety V 𝒦, then so does the lift of 𝑨.  Let us get the tedious proof of this technical lemma out of the way.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="6430" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="6435" href="Prelude.Lifts.html#2741" class="Module">Lift</a>
<a id="VlA"></a><a id="6440" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6440" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="6444" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6446" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6447" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6447" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6449" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6451" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="6459" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6461" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6462" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6462" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6464" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6466" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="6471" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6472" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6480" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6447" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6482" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6483" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6485" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6486" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝓞</a> <a id="6488" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="6490" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#542" class="Bound">𝓥</a> <a id="6492" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="6494" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6447" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6496" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="6497" class="Symbol">)}</a>
      <a id="6506" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6507" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6507" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6509" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6511" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6519" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6520" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6523" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6447" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6524" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6526" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6527" class="Symbol">}</a>

      <a id="6558" class="Comment">---------------------------------</a>
 <a id="6593" class="Symbol">→</a>    <a id="6598" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4673" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="6607" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6507" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6609" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6610" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6613" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6447" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6615" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="6616" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6618" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="6620" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4593" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="6621" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6622" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6447" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6623" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6625" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6628" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6447" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6630" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="6631" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6633" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6462" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

<a id="6636" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6440" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="6640" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6641" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4689" class="InductiveConstructor">vbase</a><a id="6646" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6647" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6647" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6648" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6650" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6650" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6651" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6653" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6655" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5353" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="6661" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6662" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4689" class="InductiveConstructor">vbase</a> <a id="6668" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6650" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6669" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6671" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6672" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6514" class="Function">lift-alg-associative</a> <a id="6693" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6647" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6694" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="7768" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7726" class="Function">vlA</a> <a id="7772" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7772" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="7774" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7776" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6440" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="7780" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7781" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7504" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7783" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7784" href="Prelude.Lifts.html#2815" class="Field">lower</a> <a id="7790" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7772" class="Bound">i</a><a id="7791" class="Symbol">))</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="closure-properties">Closure properties</a>

The types defined above represent operators with useful closure properties. We now prove a handful of such properties that we need later.

First, `P` is a closure operator.  This is proved by checking that `P` is *monotone*, *expansive*, and *idempotent*. The meaning of these terms will be clear from the definitions of the types that follow.

<pre class="Agda">

</pre>

Similarly, S is a closure operator.  The facts that S is idempotent and expansive won't be needed below, so we omit these, but we will make use of monotonicity of S.  Here is the proof of the latter.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="9984" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9842" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9991" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9991" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9995" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9996" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3099" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a><a id="10001" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10002" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10002" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="10003" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10005" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10005" class="Bound">x</a><a id="10006" class="Symbol">)</a>         <a id="10016" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10018" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3099" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a> <a id="10024" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10025" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9842" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="10032" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9991" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="10036" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10005" class="Bound">x</a><a id="10037" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="10098" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9842" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="10105" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10105" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="10109" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10110" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3243" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a><a id="10115" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10116" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10116" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="10117" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10119" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10119" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="10120" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10122" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10122" class="Bound">sA</a> <a id="10125" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10125" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="10128" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10130" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10132" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3243" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a> <a id="10138" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10139" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9842" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="10146" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10105" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="10150" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10122" class="Bound">sA</a><a id="10152" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10154" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10125" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="10158" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9842" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="10165" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10165" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="10169" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10170" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3307" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="10175" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10175" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="10177" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10177" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="10179" class="Symbol">)</a>          <a id="10190" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10192" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3307" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="10197" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10198" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9842" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="10205" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10165" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="10209" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10175" class="Bound">x</a><a id="10210" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10212" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10177" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

We sometimes want to go back and forth between our two representations of subalgebras of algebras in a class. The tools `subalgebra→S` and `S→subalgebra` are made for that purpose.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="10424" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="10431" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10431" class="Module">_</a> <a id="10433" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10434" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10434" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10436" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10436" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="10438" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10440" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="10448" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10450" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10450" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="10452" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10454" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="10459" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10460" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10468" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10434" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10470" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="10471" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="10473" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10476" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10434" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10477" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="10480" class="Keyword">where</a>

</pre>

Next we observe that lifting to a higher universe does not break the property of being a subalgebra of an algebra of a class.  In other words, if we lift a subalgebra of an algebra in a class, the result is still a subalgebra of an algebra in the class.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="lift-alg-subP"></a><a id="12470" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12470" class="Function">lift-alg-subP</a> <a id="12484" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12486" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12487" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12487" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="12489" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12489" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="12491" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12493" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="12501" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12503" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12503" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="12505" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12507" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="12512" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12513" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="12521" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12487" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="12523" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="12524" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="12526" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="12529" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12487" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="12530" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="12533" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12533" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="12535" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12537" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="12545" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12487" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="12547" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="12548" class="Symbol">}</a>

The next lemma would be too obvious to care about were it not for the fact that we'll need it later, so it too must be formalized.

We need to formalize one more lemma before arriving the main objective of this section, which is the proof of the inclusion PS⊆SP.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="lemPS⊆SP"></a><a id="14673" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14673" class="Function">lemPS⊆SP</a> <a id="14682" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14684" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14685" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14685" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="14687" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14687" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="14689" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14691" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="14699" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14701" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14701" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="14703" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14705" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="14710" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14711" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="14719" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14685" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="14721" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="14722" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="14724" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="14727" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14685" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14728" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="14731" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14731" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="14735" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14737" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a> <a id="14745" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14687" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="14747" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14685" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14748" class="Symbol">}</a>
 <a id="14751" class="Symbol">→</a>         <a id="14761" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14762" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14762" class="Bound">I</a> <a id="14764" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14766" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14687" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="14768" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a><a id="14769" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14771" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14771" class="Bound">ℬ</a> <a id="14773" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14775" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14762" class="Bound">I</a> <a id="14777" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14779" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="14787" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14685" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="14789" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="14790" class="Symbol">}</a>
 <a id="14793" class="Symbol">→</a>         <a id="14803" class="Symbol">(∀</a> <a id="14806" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14806" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="14808" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14810" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14811" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14771" class="Bound">ℬ</a> <a id="14813" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14806" class="Bound">i</a><a id="14814" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14816" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3791" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="14836" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14701" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="14837" class="Symbol">)</a>
           <a id="14850" class="Comment">-------------------------------------</a>
 <a id="14889" class="Symbol">→</a>         <a id="14899" href="Algebras.Products.html#908" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="14901" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14771" class="Bound">ℬ</a> <a id="14903" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3791" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="14923" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14924" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3644" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="14925" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14926" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14685" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14927" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14929" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14687" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="14930" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14932" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14701" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="14933" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="15608" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15592" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="15610" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15612" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3941" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a> <a id="15618" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="15621" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15621" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="15623" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15625" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8935" class="Function">P-expa</a> <a id="15632" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15633" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13569" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="15635" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13651" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="15639" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13647" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="15641" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14966" class="Bound">B≤K</a> <a id="15645" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15621" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="15647" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13647" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="15649" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13569" class="Function Operator">∣</a><a id="15650" class="Symbol">))</a>


</pre>



#### <a id="PS-in-SP">PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we are in a position to prove that a product of subalgebras of algebras in a class 𝒦 is a subalgebra of a product of algebras in 𝒦.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="PS⊆SP"></a><a id="15866" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15866" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="15872" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15874" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15875" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15875" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="15877" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15879" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="15887" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="15889" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15889" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="15891" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15893" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="15898" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15899" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="15907" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15875" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="15909" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="15910" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="15912" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="15915" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15875" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15916" class="Symbol">)}(</a><a id="15919" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15919" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="15923" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15925" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a> <a id="15933" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15934" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="15937" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15875" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15938" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="15940" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="15943" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15875" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15944" class="Symbol">))</a>
 <a id="15948" class="Symbol">→</a>      <a id="15955" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3644" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="15956" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15957" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="15960" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15875" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15961" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="15963" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="15966" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15875" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15967" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15969" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15970" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2944" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="15971" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15972" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15875" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15973"   <a id="16953" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16953" class="Function">η</a> <a id="16955" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16957" href="Algebras.Products.html#908" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="16959" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16803" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="16961" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3791" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="16981" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16982" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3644" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="16983" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16984" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16987" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16783" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16988" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16990" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16993" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16783" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16994" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16996" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16997" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3644" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="16998" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16999" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16783" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17000" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17002" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17005" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16783" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17006" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17008" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16786" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="17009" class="Symbol">))</a>
  <a id="17014" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16953" class="Function">η</a> <a id="17016" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17018" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14673" class="Function">lemPS⊆SP</a><a id="17026" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17027" class="Argument">𝓤</a> <a id="17029" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17031" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17034" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16783" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17035" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17037" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17040" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16783" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17041" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17043" class="Argument">𝒦</a> <a id="17045" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17047" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17048" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3644" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="17050" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16786" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="17051" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="17054" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16789" class="Bound">hfe</a><a id="17057" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17059" class="Argument">I</a> <a id="17061" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17063" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16800" class="Bound">I</a><a id="17064" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17066" class="Argument">ℬ</a> <a id="17068" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17070" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16803" class="Bound">𝒜</a><a id="17071" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17073" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16856" class="Function">ξ</a>

<a id="17133" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15866" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="17139" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17139" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="17143" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17144" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4187" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a><a id="17149" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17150" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17150" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17151" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17153" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17153" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="17154" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17156" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17156" class="Bound">pA</a> <a id="17159" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17159" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="17162" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17164" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17166" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3307" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="17171" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17172" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15866" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="17178" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17139" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="17182" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17156" class="Bound">pA</a><a id="17184" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17186" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17159" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="more-class-inclusions">More class inclusions</a>

We conclude this subsection with three more inclusion relations that will have bit parts to play later (e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem).

<a id="18013" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17778" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18018" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18019" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3243" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a><a id="18024" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18025" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18025" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18026" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18028" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18028" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="18029" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18031" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18031" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="18035" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18035" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="18038" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18040" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18042" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5044" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="18049" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18050" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17778" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18055" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18031" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="18058" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18060" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18035" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="18064" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17778" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18069" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18070" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3307" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="18075" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18075" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18077" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18077" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="18079" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18081" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18083" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5353" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="18089" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18090" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17778" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18095" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18075" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18096" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18098" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18077" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

We just proved that `SP(𝒦) ⊆ V(𝒦)`, and we did so under fairly general assumptions about the universe level parameters.  Unfortunately, this is sometimes not quite general enough, so we now prove the inclusion again for the specific universe parameters that align with subsequent applications of this result.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="SP⊆V&#39;"></a><a id="18438" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18438" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18444" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18446" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18447" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18447" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18449" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18451" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="18459" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18461" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18461" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18463" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18465" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18470" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18471" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18479" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18447" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18481" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18482" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18484" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18485" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18488" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18447" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18489" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="18493" class="Symbol">→</a>      <a id="18500" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2944" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="18501" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18502" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18505" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18447" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18506" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18508" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18511" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18447" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18513" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="18514" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18516" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18517" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3644" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="18518" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18519" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18447" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18520" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18522" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18525" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18447" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18526" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18528" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18461" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18529" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18531" href="Relations.Unary.html#2280" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="18533" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4593" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="18535" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18461" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

<a id="18538" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18438" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18544" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18545" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3042" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a><a id="18550" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18551" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18551" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18552" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18554" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18554" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18555" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18557" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18559" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5353" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="18565" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18566" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6440" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="18570" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18571" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17778" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18576" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18577" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3042" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="18583" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18554" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18584" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="18588" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18589" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2988" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="18595" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18596" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6514" class="Function">lift-alg-associative</a> <a id="18617" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18551" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18618" class="Symbol">))</a>
<a id="18621" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18438" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18627" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18628" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3099" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a> <a id="18634" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18634" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18635" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18637" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18639" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6440" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="18643" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18644" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17778" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18649" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18634" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18650" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="18653" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18438" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18659" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18660" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18660" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18661" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="18663" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3164" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a><a id="18667" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18668" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18668" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18669" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18671" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18671" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="18672" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18674" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18674" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="18678" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18678" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="18681" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18683" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18685" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5044" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="18692" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18693" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6440" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="18697" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18698" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17778" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18703" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18674" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="18706" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18709" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18723" class="Function">B≤lA</a>
 <a id="18715" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="18723" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18723" class="Function">B≤lA</a> <a id="18728" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18730" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18671" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="18732" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3598" class="Function Operator">≤</a> <a id="18734" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4673" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="18743" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18668" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18745" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18746" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18749" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18660" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18751" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="18752" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="18756" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18723" class="Function">B≤lA</a> <a id="18761" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18763" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18764" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#7364" class="Function">lift-alg-lower-≤-lift</a> <a id="18786" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18671" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="18788" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18789" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18668" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18790" class="Symbol">})</a> <a id="18793" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18678" class="Bound">B≤A</a>

<a id="18798" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18438" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18804" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18805" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3243" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a> <a id="18811" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18811" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="18815" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18815" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="18818" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18820" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18822" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5044" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="18829" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18830" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18438" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18836" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18811" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="18839" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18841" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18815" class="Bound">B≤A</a>

<a id="18846" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18438" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18852" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18853" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18853" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18854" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18856" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18856" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18857" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="18859" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3307" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a><a id="18863" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18864" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18864" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18865" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18867" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18867" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="18868" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18870" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18870" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18872" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18872" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="18875" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18877" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18879" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5353" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="18885" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18886" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6440" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="18890" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18891" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17778" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18896" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18870" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18897" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18900" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18911" class="Function">γ</a>

  <a id="18911" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18911" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="18913" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18915" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4673" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="18924" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18864" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18926" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18927" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18930" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18853" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18932" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="18933" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18935" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1151" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="18937" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18867" class="Bound">𝑩</a>
  <a id="18941" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18911" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="18943" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18945" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4495" class="Function">Trans-≅</a> <a id="18953" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18954" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4673" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="18963" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18864" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18965" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18966" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18969" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18853" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18971" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="18972" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18975" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18867" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="18977" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18978" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2988" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="18984" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4959" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="18994" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18996" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18872" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="S-in-SP">⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we prove a result that plays an important role, e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem. As we saw in [Algebras.Products][], the (informal) product `⨅ S(𝒦)` of all subalgebras of algebras in 𝒦 is implemented (formally) in the [UALib][] as `⨅ 𝔄 S(𝒦)`. Our goal is to prove that this product belongs to `SP(𝒦)`. We do so by first proving that the product belongs to `PS(𝒦)` and then applying the `PS⊆SP` lemma.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="class-prod-s-∈-ps"></a><a id="19496" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19496" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="19514" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19516" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19517" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19517" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19519" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19521" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="19529" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19531" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19531" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="19533" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19535" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19517" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19537" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a><a id="19538" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19540" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19540" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19542" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19544" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="19549" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19550" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19558" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19517" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19560" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19561" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19563" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19566" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19517" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19567" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="19571" class="Symbol">→</a>                  <a id="19590" href="Algebras.Products.html#3936" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="19604" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19605" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19517" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19606" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19608" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19517" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19609" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19611" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19531" class="Bound">X</a><a id="19612" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19614" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19615" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2944" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19617" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19540" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19618" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19620" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="19622" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19623" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3644" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="19624" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19625" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19628" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19517" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19629" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19631" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19634" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19517" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19635" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19637" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19638" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2944" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19640" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19540" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19641" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="19645" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19496" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="19663" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19664" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19664" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19665" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19667" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19667" class="Bound">X</a><a id="19668" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19670" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19670" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19671" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="19674" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19676" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4107" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a> <a id="19682" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19950" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="19689" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19690" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6804" class="Function">⨅≅</a> <a id="19693" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#545" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="19697" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20001" class="Function">llA≅A</a><a id="19702" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="19705" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="19713" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19713" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="19716" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19716" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="19720" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19722" href="Algebras.Products.html#2792" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="19724" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19725" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2944" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19727" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19670" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19728" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19730" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19732" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19740" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19741" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19744" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19664" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19745" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19747" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
